<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:carmen.html>carmen</a> (5597)</h1><br></body> 
***carmine.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:carmine.html>carmine</a> (12481)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">carmin</i>, from irregular <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">carminium</i>, itself from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">قِرْمِز</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qirmiz</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crimson, kermes</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from Sanskrit <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">कृमिज</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kṛmija</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">produced by <a href = vnd.unilang:worms.html>worms</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">कृमि</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kṛ́mi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">worm, insect</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), plus or with influence from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">minium</i>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">crimson</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">kermes</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:carmine.html>carmine</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:carmines.html>carmines</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A purplish-red pigment, made from dye obtained from the cochineal beetle; carminic acid or any of its derivatives.
<ul><li><b>1967</b>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Time_(magazine)" class="extiw" title="w:Time (magazine)">Time</a></i>, "The Case of the Dubious Dye," 6 January, 1967, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.time.com/time/magazine/article/0,9171,843172,00.html">[1]</a>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>Cases</a> of cubana salmonellosis in three other states <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> traced to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:carmine.html>carmine</a></b> red, and supplies <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> called in. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> But authorities have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> checking other <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a> for <b><a href = vnd.unilang:carmine.html>carmine</a></b> red, knowing that it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a favorite coloring in candy, chewing gum, ice cream, cough syrups and <a href = vnd.unilang:drugs.html>drugs</a>. Manufacturers like to use it because of a legal quirk: being a natural rather than a synthetic product, it does not have to be mentioned on <a href = vnd.unilang:labels.html>labels</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A purplish-red colour, resembling that pigment.
<ul><li><b>1854</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_David_Thoreau" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry David Thoreau"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> David Thoreau</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Walden">Walden</a></i>, New York: Thomas Y. Crowell amp; Co., 1910, Chapter XIV, p. 347, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/walden01thor">[2]</a>
<dl><dd>He wore a great coat in midsummer, being affected with the trembling <a href = vnd.unilang:delirium.html>delirium</a>, and his face <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the color of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:carmine.html>carmine</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li>c. <b>1862</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emily_Dickinson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Emily Dickinson">Emily Dickinson</a>, in <i>The Complete Poems of Emily Dickinson</i>, edited by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_H._Johnson_(scholar)" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas H. Johnson (scholar)">Thomas H. Johnson</a>, Boston: Little, Brown amp; Co., 1960, pp. 225-6,
<dl><dd>I am Alive—I guess— / The <a href = vnd.unilang:branches.html>Branches</a> on my Hand / Are full of Morning Glory— / And at my finger's end— / The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:carmine.html>Carmine</a></b>—tingles warm—</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1920</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/F._Scott_Fitzgerald" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:F. Scott Fitzgerald">F. Scott Fitzgerald</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/This_Side_of_Paradise" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:This Side of Paradise">This Side of Paradise</a></i>, Chapter 5, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/files/805/805-h/805-h.htm">[3]</a>
<dl><dd>He pictured himself in an adobe house in Mexico, half-reclining on a rug-covered couch, his slender, artistic <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a> closed on a cigarette while he listened to guitars strumming melancholy undertones to an age-old dirge of Castile and an olive-skinned, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:carmine.html>carmine</a></b>-lipped girl caressed his hair.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1938</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_Orwell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:George Orwell">George Orwell</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Homage_to_Catalonia" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Homage to Catalonia">Homage to Catalonia</a></i>, Chapter 4, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.net.au/ebooks02/0201111h.html">[4]</a>
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> the dawn breaking behind the hill-tops in our rear, the first narrow streaks of gold, like swords slitting the darkness, and then the growing light and the <a href = vnd.unilang:seas.html>seas</a> of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:carmine.html>carmine</a></b> cloud stretching away into inconceivable <a href = vnd.unilang:distances.html>distances</a> <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1987</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Toni_Morrison" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Toni Morrison"><a href = vnd.unilang:toni.html>Toni</a> Morrison</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beloved_(novel)" class="extiw" title="w:Beloved (novel)">Beloved</a></i>, New York: Vintage, 2004, p. 33,
<dl><dd>The velvet I seen <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> brown, but in Boston they got all colors. <b><a href = vnd.unilang:carmine.html>Carmine</a></b>. That means red but when you talk about velvet you got to say '<b><a href = vnd.unilang:carmine.html>carmine</a></b>.'</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:carmine.html>carmine</a> colour: <span style="background-color:7F3A3F; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">pigment</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">crimson</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">cochineal</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">C.I. 75470</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">E120</span></li></ul>

***carnaval.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:carnaval.html>carnaval</a> (14466)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:carnaval.html>carnaval</a></i>, either from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">carnivale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">carnelevale</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">carnem</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flesh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">levāre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lighten, raise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The alternative <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">carnem</i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vale</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flesh farewell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a folk etymology.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:carnaval.html>carnaval</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:carnavals.html>carnavals</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:carnaval.html>carnavalletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The carnival, last festive occasion(s) before Lent, notably on Shrove Tuesday</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">within the southern Netherlands and Belgium, specifically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A festival celebrated with costuming, <a href = vnd.unilang:parades.html>parades</a> and other festivities, with a general emphasis on parody, jest and local tradition and dialect.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in some areas</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">vastenavond</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:carnivoor.html>carnivoor</a> (42486)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">carnivorus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flesh-eating</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">carō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flesh, meat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vorāre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to devour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***caro.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:caro.html>caro</a> (57906)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Italic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Italic language">Proto-Italic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="itc-pro">*karō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ker-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)ker-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheren.html>scheren</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:scheren.html>scheren</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">skjære</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">skära</i>; and (<i>from Indo-European</i>) with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κείρω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">keírō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I cut off</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shear</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">harr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut, to mow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">skìrti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">separate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">ysgar</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">separate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sharp</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la">carō</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">carnis</b>); <i>third declension</i>
</p>
<ol><li>flesh, meat</li>
<li>pulp of a fruit</li>
<li>body</li></ol>

***carousel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:carousel.html>carousel</a> (94712)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:carrousel.html>carrousel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">carosello</i>, probably from <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">carro</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">carrus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:carousel.html>carousel</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">carousels</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A merry-go-round <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">type of ride on rotating platform</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
<ul><li><b>1951</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/J.D._Salinger" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:J.D. Salinger">J.D. Salinger</a>, <i>The Catcher in the Rye</i>, Chapter 25:
<dl><dd>That's one nice thing about <b><a href = vnd.unilang:carrousel.html>carrousels</a></b><sup style="font-style:normal">[<i>sic</i>]</sup>, they always play the same song.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A continuously revolving device for item delivery.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">After collecting his suitcase at the baggage <b><a href = vnd.unilang:carousel.html>carousel</a></b>, he left the airport.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>The rotating glass plate in a microwave <a href = vnd.unilang:oven.html>oven</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">graphical user interface</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A visual component that <a href = vnd.unilang:displays.html>displays</a> a horizontal series of <a href = vnd.unilang:items.html>items</a> one at a time.</li>
<li>An equestrian discipline in which groups of <a href = vnd.unilang:riders.html>riders</a> make various formations.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tilting match or tournament accompanied by games, <a href = vnd.unilang:shows.html>shows</a>, and allegorical performances.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:carousel.html>carousel</a> voting</span></li></ul>
</body>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:carpaccio.html>carpaccio</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:carpaccio.html>carpaccio</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>

***carvel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:carvel.html>carvel</a> (84416)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:carvel.html>carvel</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">carvelle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">carvile</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:kervel.html>kervel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small ship; caravel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">caruelle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">carvelle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">kirvelle</i>,<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> see further at <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">caravel</i>. The English word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">karveel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:carvel.html>carvel</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">carvels</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Synonym of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">caravel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a light, usually lateen-rigged sailing ship</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>The sea <a href = vnd.unilang:blubber.html>blubber</a> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Cyanea_capillata" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Cyanea capillata"><i>Cyanea capillata</i></a></span>); <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A jellyfish (<i>Medusozoa</i>).</li></ol>

***casserole.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:casserole.html>casserole</a> (70680)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:casserole.html>casserole</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:casserole.html>casserole</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">casseroles</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A dish of glass or earthenware, with a <a href = vnd.unilang:lid.html>lid</a>, in which food <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> baked and sometimes served.</li>
<li>Food, such as a stew, cooked in such a dish.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">glass or earthenward dish</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:casserole.html>casserole</a> dish</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:castraat.html>castraat</a> (118859)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">castrato</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">castrō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to castrate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, likely from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caedō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:castraat.html>castraat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:castraten.html>castraten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:castraat.html>castraatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A castrato, male who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> castrated, surgically emasculated.</li>
<li>Notably a castrated singer (usually a (former) treble chorister).</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">castrato</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">gecastreerde</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontmannen.html>ontmande</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">castraatzanger</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:castratie.html>castratie</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:castreren.html>castreren</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:castraat.html>castraat</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li>gecastreerde <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:dier.html>dier</a>.</li>
<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:muziek.html>muziek</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:mannelijke.html>mannelijke</a> sopraan- of altzanger, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevolg.html>gevolg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jeugdige.html>jeugdige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:castratie.html>castratie</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> jongensstem <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:behouden.html>behouden</a>.
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeventiende.html>zeventiende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eeuw.html>eeuw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zongen.html>zongen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:castraten.html>castraten</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Sixtijnse <a href = vnd.unilang:kapel.html>kapel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> sopraanstemmen.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***castreren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:castreren.html>castreren</a> (21988)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:castreren.html>castreren</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">castrō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:castreren.html>castreren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to castrate, to neuter (remove the testicles of)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remove the female genitals, or <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> a plant's stamen</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to emasculate, to reduce to a lesser, weaker state ('less <a href = vnd.unilang:balls.html>balls</a>')</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remove contentious material (from a text, <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a>, etc.); to censor, to bowdlerize, to redact</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mutilate oneself, physically or otherwise</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:castraat.html>castraat</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:castratie.html>castratie</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:castreren.html>castreren</a></b>
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cāsus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chance, event</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cadō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fall, happen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<li>A coincidence.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toeval.html>toeval</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***catfish.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a> (94695)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cat</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fish</i>. Likely so named for its prominent barbels like a cat's <a href = vnd.unilang:whiskers.html>whiskers</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">catfishes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>any fish of the order Siluriformes, mainly found in fresh water, lacking scales, and having barbels like <a href = vnd.unilang:whiskers.html>whiskers</a> around the mouth
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">catlet</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Africa</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">sheat</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">sheatfish</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">catfishes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">catfishing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">catfished</b>)

<ol><li>To fish for <a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a></a>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the 2010 documentary <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catfish_(film)" class="extiw" title="w:Catfish (film)"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>Catfish</a></a></i>, supposedly inspired by the practice of fishermen <a href = vnd.unilang:keeping.html>keeping</a> cod active by <a href = vnd.unilang:storing.html>storing</a> them with <a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a> (see sense 1) which nip at their <a href = vnd.unilang:tails.html>tails</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">catfishes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Internet</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone who creates a fake profile on a social media platform in order to deceive people.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Internet</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Such a fake profile.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">catfishes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">catfishing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">catfished</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Internet<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To create and operate a fake online profile to deceive (someone).
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> January 17,  <a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> Pilon,  “In <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a>’<a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a> Story, Deception Ripped From the Screen”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_New_York_Times" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The New York Times">The New York Times</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2013/01/18/sports/ncaafootball/deception-ripped-from-the-screen-in-hoax-story-of-manti-teo.html">[1]</a></sup>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Standard_Serial_Number" class="extiw" title="w:International Standard Serial Number">ISSN</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.worldcat.org/issn/0362-4331">0362-4331</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Getting <b>catfished</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> when someone falls for a person online who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not necessarily real. It can involve pictures, phone calls, social media profiles, text messages, e-mails and <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> phony friends or family members.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b> January 16,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Donald_Glover" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Donald Glover">Donald <a href = vnd.unilang:glover.html>Glover</a></a> as <a href = vnd.unilang:troy.html>Troy</a>,  <cite>Cooperative Polygraphy</cite> ('<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Community_(TV_series)" class="extiw" title="w:Community (TV series)">Community</a>'), season 5, episode 4, NBC, 12:17 from the start:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><i>[to Abed]</i> You made a profile for a fake dude and lured her into an online relationship. <i>[to Annie]</i> He's <b>catfishing</b> you.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><span class="see-cites">For more quotations using this term, see Citations:<a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a>.</span></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cat</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">walk</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:catwalk.html>catwalk</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:catwalks.html>catwalks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An elevated enclosed passage providing access fore and aft from the bridge of a merchant vessel.</li>
<li>Any similar elevated walkway.</li>

***caviar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:caviar.html>caviar</a> (84395)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:caviar.html>caviar</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">caviaro</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">خاویار</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">havyar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">havyar</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">خاویار</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xâvyâr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">خایه</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xâye</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">egg</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">egg</i>). Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ajvar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:caviar.html>caviar</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">caviars</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Roe of the sturgeon or other large fish, considered a delicacy.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something whose flavour <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> too fine for the vulgar taste.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:caviar.html>caviar</a> to the general</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cowboy.html>cowboy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:caviar.html>caviar</a></span></li></ul>
</body> 
***cavil.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a> (37322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">caviller</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mock, jest, rail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cavillor</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jeer, mock, satirise, reason captiously</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cavilla</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jeering, raillery, scoffing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">cavillare</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">cavillar</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">cavilar</i>; nominal usage developed within English from the original verbal usage.<sup id="cite_ref-OED_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-OED-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">cavils</b>, <i>present participle</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cavilling</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">caviling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cavilled</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">caviled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To criticise for petty or frivolous reasons.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">be hypercritical</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">nitpick</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">pettifog</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">split hairs</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1598?</b>, William Shakespeare, <i>Two <a href = vnd.unilang:gentlemen.html>Gentlemen</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:verona.html>Verona</a></i>, Act I, scene I:
<dl><dd>'<a href = vnd.unilang:tis.html>Tis</a> love you <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a></b> at: I am not Love.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Barr_(writer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Barr (writer)">Robert Barr</a>,  chapter 5, in  <cite>Lord Stranleigh Abroad</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL1796924W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Stranleigh found no difficulty in getting a cavalcade together at Bleacher’s station, an amazingly long distance west of New York. A <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> finds little trouble in obtaining what he wants, if he never <b>cavils</b> at the price asked, and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> willing to pay in advance.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1928</b>,  D. H. Lawrence,  <cite>Lady Chatterley's Lover</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I wish you wouldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hilda.html>Hilda</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1976</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Richard_Dawkins" class="extiw" title="w:Richard Dawkins">Richard Dawkins</a>,  <cite>The Selfish Gene</cite>, Kindle edition, OUP Oxford, published 2016, page 368:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But their first supporting quotation, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <i>The Selfish Gene</i>, includes selfish genes that do have phenotypic <a href = vnd.unilang:effects.html>effects</a>. Far it be from <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, however, to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a></b> at the honour of being quoted in the <i>Oxford English Dictionary</i>!</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">cavils</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A petty or trivial objection or criticism.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1835</b>,  Charles G. Finney,  <cite>Lectures on revivals of religion</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not worth while to spend your time in arguing against a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a></b>, but make him feel he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> committing a sin to plead it, and thus enlist his conscience on your side.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>
